    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

<span id="freeTextContainer10529743417101325474"><b>4 Sexy Stars.</b>	<br/><br/>In this second book, previous womanizer Seth is now in love and trying to make his relationship with Olivia work. <br/>Both seeking happiness with the other they are settled on making it work, but things aren’t always as we want them to be. Fights, ex-lovers, their own past and a previous enemy established on ruining Seth will all of them get in the way of their love and they have to find out if they love each other enough to fight against all of that. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391558086ra/8410475.gif' width='400' height='250' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was better than the firs</span>
  <span id="freeText10529743417101325474" style="display:none"><b>4 Sexy Stars.</b>	<br><br>In this second book, previous womanizer Seth is now in love and trying to make his relationship with Olivia work. <br>Both seeking happiness with the other they are settled on making it work, but things aren’t always as we want them to be. Fights, ex-lovers, their own past and a previous enemy established on ruining Seth will all of them get in the way of their love and they have to find out if they love each other enough to fight against all of that. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1391558086ra/8410475.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was better than the first one and I felt more connected with the characters. Their relationship felt more real and although there was some little annoyances I still liked it.<br>If you’re into MMA fighters (and I know you are *wink*), you have to give these books a try. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388683472i/7901653.jpg" width="350" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br> <b>Rating: </b> 4 Stars. <br> <b>Storyline: </b> Predictable at a lot of moments, but sweet and entertaining. <br> <b>Writing Style: </b> First person, dual POV. Appealing. <br> <b>Character Development: </b> Seth was a pretty loveable alpha-male, even that sometimes some of his attitudes pissed me off. Olivia is “meh”. Her lack of professionalism that annoyed me in the first book is still there and I really can’t get over it. I don’t like unprofessional people, at all! And Selena is a bitch and probably the worst friend ever. Yeah, that’s all. <br> <b>Steam: </b> Hot. <br> <b>HEA: </b>	<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Yes. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer719373492" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3772293573247929856">I couldn't wait to write my review because I knew how nervous Skyla was about this book. She had zero reason to be. <br/><br/>Authors, take note. THIS is how you write a second book. There was no needless drama. No stupid actions. Just 2 people in a relationship making it work. It was also HOT as HELL. I loved every minute. <br/><br/><br/>I know some people love Remy. From this moment forward my #1 MMA guy will always be Seth. <br/><br/>I'm looking forward to the next book!</span>

          </span>
        </div>

And will these lovers get their HEA? <i>Read and you will find out!</i><br><br><b>
  <i>Too Consumed,</i>
</b> was a lovely read and did not disappoint me in any way. I liked how both Seth and Olivia are flawed in their own way and yet they are what each other needs in their lives.<br><br>Both characters have their own set of issues and uncertainties that they battle throughout the course of the story and it’s interesting to see how it all turns out. I’m not saying that it’s all hearts and rainbows throughout this because it’s not. Often at times, when these obstacles did happen, I wanted to slam both of their heads together because they were so stubborn!! Seth is very aggressive and head on whereas Olivia could be the same when provoked but is naturally more timid and reserved. <i>Very interesting combination wouldn’t you say?</i> Especially, when you see how they work things out and confront things of past and present.<br><br><b>An exemplary and steamy read!!</b> Pheew! *fans self* Definitely worth waiting for!! I now can’t wait for <b>
  <i>Forever Consumed</i>
</b> which looks like to be the final installment in their story!!<br></span>

<div id="review_882174195" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/882174195" />
    <a title="Marci" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14107900-marci"><img alt="Marci" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1491518040p2/14107900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/882174195?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marci" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marci" href="/user/show/14107900-marci">Marci</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14107900-marci?shelf=read-2014">read-2014</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer882174195" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12929050624249075460">Yikes, review to come, took me twice as long to read this as it normally would, so I need to get my thoughts straight.<br/><br/>So, looking back through my review of the first book, Consumed, it appears I rated it 3 to 3.5-stars, and I cannot for the life of me figure out how that could be after reading book two. To say I am frustrated would be putting it mildly. It took me forever to read this book. The writing was ok, what I was reading was just boring and not very interesting, honestly. <br/><br/>Olivia was stil</span>
  <span id="freeText12929050624249075460" style="display:none">Yikes, review to come, took me twice as long to read this as it normally would, so I need to get my thoughts straight.<br /><br />So, looking back through my review of the first book, Consumed, it appears I rated it 3 to 3.5-stars, and I cannot for the life of me figure out how that could be after reading book two. To say I am frustrated would be putting it mildly. It took me forever to read this book. The writing was ok, what I was reading was just boring and not very interesting, honestly. <br /><br />Olivia was still annoying and not a very likable character with all her self righteousness. If she were a real person I would probably want to punch her in her smug face. I really cannot get a grasp on why I am supposed to care about the person she was on the pages of this book. She gives her friend, Selena crap about the sexual adventures between Selena and Jackson, then turns around and enjoys the same type of things here and there,with Seth. What makes it wrong when others do it, but okay when she does? I thought her actions after Don paid a surprise visit to Seth was ridiculously stupid. The fact that Jackson went along with it was idiotic. I do not blame Seth for being upset with her, and was glad when other characters were telling her she was in the wrong. Yet she still tried to maintain an air of righteousness about the situation, it was maddening. Also, what is the deal with moving in with her mom after being so adamant about NOT moving back in book one? Yes, I know her dad dies in book one, and I get maybe staying with her temporarily, but moving in completely is nutty considering the fight it had been. I don't like her. I mean, thoughout the book she is such a snooty witch. It was present through the entire book. After Seth's first fight in Vegas, she declines going out with everyone, says she is going to stay at home and read?! What a bitchy thing to do. Go out with everyone, jeez. I don't care if going out ends up being a debacle, this is a time you suck it up and just go. If you are worried about being selfish, well, sister, this is you being selfish by not going this particular time.<br /><br />Seth, well, he started reminding me of Nico in Worth the Fight and I honestly was getting the backstory of Seth and Olivia mixed up with Nico and Elle. I read Consumed in November 2013 and Worth the Fight in February 2014, and I have to say I really think they were quite similar, and I could have interchanged characters very easily. There was also the ending with the fight with Don that reminded me of another MMA book, but dont know which one, I think it was Remy. All of these MMA books are really similar and starting to get confused in my mind, I don't think a whole lot of new scenarios are coming up in these books to make them unique. <br /><br />I like Seth, he seems to really love Olivia and be amazed at the amount of love he has for her and how much she seems to center him, he welcomes that. But I felt his character sounded soft and gooey one minute, then was overly cocky the next. It got to be quite obnoxious, and the demands he was making to his new employer was way over the top. Who is he that he is be the newest member of this pro fighting league and tell them what is going to happen? I was actually glad to see the organization standing up to him. So, he demands certain things with his new employer, yet he cannot ask Olivia to marry him? What? If he is as cocky as he is portrayed to be, this should not be an issue. Yes, I get Olivia kind of unravels his tough guy facade a bit, but whatever, it makes no sense. <br /><br />There was a common theme for both Olivia and Seth for awhile. They both kept asking themselves if they were selfish or selfless. Who the hell cares, you were both annoying the hell out of me. There was soooooo much internal rambling by both characters I thought I was going to go mad. It took forever to get to Vegas, I think it was 6-days until Vegas when the book starts, and that timeframe took like 65% of the book and the 4-WEEKS they were actually in Vegas took like 30% of the book. Just what we were supposed to get out of those 6-days, I am not certain. I thought this was a book about an MMA fighter and other than a few training scenes, we had 2 fights shoved in the last 10% of the book. <br /><br />BTW, the way Seth proposed? HORRIBLE!!! I though it was extremely degrading, and I was actually waiting for it to have been recorded and used by Don in some way. Maybe it will in the next book? I mean, didn't Seth say he did not enjoy or think about doing the things Jackson does, but then he does the night he proposes? Just...no.<br /><br />To stop my rambling, I am going to say that this book felt different than the first, it felt disjointed and I have no idea what the purpose of this book really was other than to get our characters married. The past flings that randomly popped up, the angry spells, the no having sex rule, all of it was silly and used as an excuse to make this into a 3-book series. I am going to make a guess and say this story, which has ultimately become as much about Seth and Don's rivalry as Seth and Olivia's relationship, could have been told in 2-books easily. I am pretty sure I am not going to read the next book. I don't care enough about any of this to go on. Sorry, I was hoping to like this, even pushed it up on my TBR list to read it, but I barely made it through.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12929050624249075460" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer1468700107152799172"><b>5 Never Want this Series to End Stars!</b><br/><br/>I'm not going to write a long review about this book because I'm too<b> impatient</b> to read the<b> next book</b> in this series! But I will say that this series has made me <b>so happy</b> and put me in a really <b>good mood</b>! So that's saying something right there <b>:)</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381209456ra/4532718.gif' width='400' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am truly <b>in love</b> with Seth even though he is a truly <b>cocky bastard</b>. He's unapologetic but has a vulnerable side to him that is so <b>endearing</b>. His <b>love</b> for Olivia is so passionate and pure; she's transformed him yet a</span>
  <span id="freeText1468700107152799172" style="display:none"><b>5 Never Want this Series to End Stars!</b><br><br>I'm not going to write a long review about this book because I'm too<b> impatient</b> to read the<b> next book</b> in this series! But I will say that this series has made me <b>so happy</b> and put me in a really <b>good mood</b>! So that's saying something right there <b>:)</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381209456ra/4532718.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am truly <b>in love</b> with Seth even though he is a truly <b>cocky bastard</b>. He's unapologetic but has a vulnerable side to him that is so <b>endearing</b>. His <b>love</b> for Olivia is so passionate and pure; she's transformed him yet also allowed him to be true to himself. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426279918i/13997263.jpg" width="250" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1382105529ra/5668492.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380376611ra/731541.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia's not judgmental of his past and isn't consumed by insecurity and jealousness, which is <b>so refreshing</b>. I actually think this is the first book where the two MC's are <b>so confident </b>in each others love and <b>dedication to each other</b>. That in itself has made this an incredibly enjoyable book for me. There's still angst and some drama, it's just not surrounding their relationship. She's my idea of a perfect heroine; <b>caring, strong, confident, </b>and<b> selfless</b>.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426279918ra/13997264.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Most of the angst in this book surrounds Seth's rival Don. He is such a <b>total, complete dick!!!</b> I hate him! He's <b>sketchy, cheap, </b>and <b>dishonorable</b>. That fight scene in the end perfectly captures what a <b>sleaze ball</b> Don is. And what kind of name is Don for a bad ass? <b>lame</b> is what. In some ways I love their rivalry because I root for Seth to <b>kick Don's ass</b> and it creates some really enjoyable drama and angst.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1417552551ra/12411513.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though I'm not a big fan of violence, I couldn't help but grip the edge of my seat during the fight matches in this book. Now, I'm not saying I dislike MMA books because I <b>love them</b>, I just usually cringe during the fight scenes. But I got <b>so anxious </b>during Seth's matches I had to see if he won! Luckily he's quite bad ass so there wasn't a lot to worry about, but I got way too invested in his success and wanting him to be unbeatable.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1426279918ra/13997265.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Okay so I wrote a longer review than I was planning, but I got <b>too caught up</b> in the <b>greatness</b> of this book ;)<br><br>Side note: Although I'm not a huge fan of rap music, I will admit I've become addicted to Seth's fight song, "We Own It" by 2 Chainz and Wiz Khalifa.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1406325412ra/10536159.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

  <span id="freeText15972087120984550325" style="display:none"><b>4 Stars!!!</b><br><br><i>
  <b>“Only she has the power to consume me, to eradicate all train of rational thinking.”</b>
</i><br><br>More interesting and definitely hotter than the first book!!! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1398756992i/9460368._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Olivia and Seth overcame many challenges in the first book but now there are facing some new ones like the reality of professional MMA and the problems couples are usually having. This is all new to them so of course there will be some (lets say) problematic situations. <br><br>Seth is jealous even from Olivia’s shadow. It’s just seriously annoying but also (a little) endearing. This is the first relationship in his life and I really enjoyed reading about his struggles. I find some of his actions quite funny! <br><br><i>
  <b>“I told you when we met that I’m fucking selfish and spoiled, and I wasn’t kidding. I want every one of your smiles, every laugh, every tear, every-fucking-thing— all of it— I want it and I want it all to myself.”</b>
</i><br><br>Olivia on the other hand is struggling with Seth’s past. It is definitely not easy to be with a guy with a past like his. Threesomes, alcohol, aggression…But she is determined not to let this ruin her happiness. She understands he is not perfect and she doesn’t want to change him. So…she tries to adapt. <br><br><i>
  <b>“He’s only human, and being human means you’re vulnerable, that you have weaknesses and imperfections. That’s the beauty of it. Being human is about making mistakes and learning from them… or not, if you don’t want to. There’s too much pressure to be perfect these days, and guess what? People are imperfect. People are annoying, stupid, and rude at times, but it’s okay.”</b>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <span id="reviewTextContainer729493568" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4566251704384327558">I finally figured out why I love Consumed, Real and Beautiful Disaster so much, it's definitely the intensity of the fighting scenes, rather it's inside or outside the ring. Hands down Too Consumed is an all-time favorite, I couldn't wait for the story to continue. Loved it!</span>

          </span>

<div id="review_817929694" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/817929694" />
    <a title="Hailey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10532998-hailey"><img alt="Hailey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1476488264p2/10532998.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/817929694?book_show_action=true">Jan 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hailey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hailey" href="/user/show/10532998-hailey">Hailey</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10532998-hailey?shelf=dropped">dropped</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10532998-hailey?shelf=anuerysm-worthy-heroine">anuerysm-worthy-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10532998-hailey?shelf=heroine-i-want-to-b-smack">heroine-i-want-to-b-smack</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10532998-hailey?shelf=gasp-heroes-i-actually-disliked">gasp-heroes-i-actually-disliked</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer817929694" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7641815937012355570">Another one I couldn't rate because I actually didn't finish the book. I just... couldn't. Tell you why in a moment. <br/>First up - props to the author for actually having Dual POV's this time! Yay - no stuck in Olivia's head for the whole book. Saying that however, I got to like 16% in and had to give up. I thought after book one maybe these characters would improve and they would just be... together if you know what I mean. You know how in some books characters are so attunted to each other they'r</span>
  <span id="freeText7641815937012355570" style="display:none">Another one I couldn't rate because I actually didn't finish the book. I just... couldn't. Tell you why in a moment. <br />First up - props to the author for actually having Dual POV's this time! Yay - no stuck in Olivia's head for the whole book. Saying that however, I got to like 16% in and had to give up. I thought after book one maybe these characters would improve and they would just be... together if you know what I mean. You know how in some books characters are so attunted to each other they're just flawless? Well sadly thiswas not to be with seth and Olivia. I know I maybe i nthe minority here but I really couldn't give a toss because I felt after everything they went through together as a couple? (if you could call them and their erratic moods that) in the first book, they would just be!<br /><br />Olivia - As soon as I started her chapter I realised how mow I just don't like her! I just don't.<br />Seth - I couldn't get a read on his character and being the male lead and after a first book, I'm guessing that's not good. I should be able to say something about him, feel something about him.<br /><br />To me, with how far into it I got, it felt a bit weird and diconnected. Seth and Olvia's scences together felt off, boring, dry, plain, bland. They were like young kids trying to figure their way around each other with the way their actions felt disjointed. I mean for a reformed man-whore and a girl who had a man-whore ex you think they would have a bit more... a bit more... *sigh* - just a bit more!<br /><br />Sorry gonna leave this series where it is - all the best to the author with her future endeavours.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7641815937012355570" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_762547432" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/762547432" />
    <a title="Shannon" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10436494-shannon"><img alt="Shannon" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1384798006p2/10436494.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/762547432?book_show_action=true">Nov 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Shannon" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Shannon" href="/user/show/10436494-shannon">Shannon</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer762547432" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17928312463672208839">This one fell a little flat for me, for some reason. <br/><br/>I loved Seth Marc and Oliva in the Consumed. I thought it was really an awesome story especially when I was already coming off my Remy high from reading 'Mine' last month.<br/><br/>So when Too Consumed came out, it was really a no brainer on picking it up and falling in love with this couple all over again.<br/><br/>But the story line didn't do much for me. In fact really nothing happened in this book at all. I mean NOTHING. <br/><br/>There is no drama between Olivia and S</span>
  <span id="freeText17928312463672208839" style="display:none">This one fell a little flat for me, for some reason. <br /><br />I loved Seth Marc and Oliva in the Consumed. I thought it was really an awesome story especially when I was already coming off my Remy high from reading 'Mine' last month.<br /><br />So when Too Consumed came out, it was really a no brainer on picking it up and falling in love with this couple all over again.<br /><br />But the story line didn't do much for me. In fact really nothing happened in this book at all. I mean NOTHING. <br /><br />There is no drama between Olivia and Seth, they are in love, he wants to marry her, she loves him.. She is dealing with life after her father passing away in book one and she is helping her mom cope. Outside of an enemy of Seth's who we met in book one.. NOTHING happens in this book. I felt often times like we were reading about a totally different couple. I needed a bit more substance, and I think that is why it took me over a week to read it.<br /><br />SO if you are wondering why I still have it 4 stars, it's because the writing is not bad, and I still loved reading about Seth and Olivia and Selena and Jackson(although we talked about them too much which makes me feel that there is a book coming out with the two of them as the MC's soon) I just felt like we were a tad bit ripped off and that this book was used as a filler for something else. I wanted to see something happen with Mason, and it in general just felt way too.. nice..</span>
  <a data-text-id="17928312463672208839" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_770124603" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/770124603" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12758001-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1366240864p2/12758001.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/770124603?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/12758001-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer770124603" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14445119215054051893"><b>Pure Realism! </b><br/><br/>Olivia has officially tamed the over confident playboy Seth Marc. And - as their relationship grows and continues in book 2,some of the obstacles they feel they have overcame, returns with a vengeance. With Seth first professional fight coming up Olivia proves to be his number one supporter.<br/><br/>Seth and Olivia were not perfect but they are perfect together. They were just as amazing in Too Consumed then in Consumed. They were physically affectionate, emotionally connected and their act</span>
  <span id="freeText14445119215054051893" style="display:none"><b>Pure Realism! </b><br><br>Olivia has officially tamed the over confident playboy Seth Marc. And - as their relationship grows and continues in book 2,some of the obstacles they feel they have overcame, returns with a vengeance. With Seth first professional fight coming up Olivia proves to be his number one supporter.<br><br>Seth and Olivia were not perfect but they are perfect together. They were just as amazing in Too Consumed then in Consumed. They were physically affectionate, emotionally connected and their actions toward each other seemed to convey a sense of peace in the other.<br><br>Most importantly for me, Seth and Olivia’s relationship including the ups and downs felt genuine, felt normal and something that you could relate to. When they are together the universe is theirs and they connect so deeply.<br><br><a href="http://s1334.photobucket.com/user/jillsstark/media/1157717_495371117220457_499530316_n_zps9de8cd3d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395197020i/8964220.jpg" alt=" photo 1157717_495371117220457_499530316_n_zps9de8cd3d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>Favorite Quotes: </b><br><br><b>Olivia</b><br><br>“It's hard to believe someone who walks around commanding so much attention with his acute cockiness, hard muscles, and tattoos would ever let someone like me bring him to his knees-and make no mistake, I bring him to his knees. I bring him to his knees, hard.”<br><br>“I can tell you I love you to the moon and back, but as far as I'm concerned, it's not enough. I can tell you I love you to the next universe and back and the distance still isn't enough to describe how I feel. I love you. I love you more than any word, any object, any emotion and any measure of distance this life can ever depict.”<br><br><b>Seth</b><br><br>“There isn’t a hold in the world that can force me to tap out. If you get me in a hold, you better be prepared to snap to snap a bone or kill me because I will not surrender. Call me stubborn, I know I am. Call me competitive or spoiled, I’m those things too, but what I am not is weak.”<br><br>“Because I love you and I‘ve never loved anyone before… I don’t want anyone else to feel how you make me feel. I told you when we met I’m ----ing selfish and spoiled, and I wasn’t kidding. I want every one of your smiles, every laugh, every tear, every- ----ing – thing- all of it-I want it and I want it all to myself.”<br><br>A perfect FIVE stars for a perfect book.<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14445119215054051893" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_722026451" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/722026451" />
    <a title="***Cheryl***" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19414420-cheryl"><img alt="***Cheryl***" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1367258444p2/19414420.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/722026451?book_show_action=true">Sep 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="***Cheryl***" class="user" itemprop="url" name="***Cheryl***" href="/user/show/19414420-cheryl">***Cheryl***</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19414420-cheryl?shelf=arc-s">arc-s</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer722026451" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8739926378832718490">What a great second book in the Consumed series!<br/><br/>The story continues where the first book ended. Seth is now preparing for his first professional fight which will take place in Las Vegas. The main focus of the story is the development of Olivia’s and Seth relationship. They both still have their own issues which haunt them. As a couple and individually they have lots of ups and down. Together they face old flames, old enemies and old insecurities. They would fight and then they would make up. I f</span>
  <span id="freeText8739926378832718490" style="display:none">What a great second book in the Consumed series!<br /><br />The story continues where the first book ended. Seth is now preparing for his first professional fight which will take place in Las Vegas. The main focus of the story is the development of Olivia’s and Seth relationship. They both still have their own issues which haunt them. As a couple and individually they have lots of ups and down. Together they face old flames, old enemies and old insecurities. They would fight and then they would make up. I found that the plot kept me hooked throughout the book, I didn’t want to put it down as I wanted to find out what happens next. <br /><br />Olivia and Seth seem to have grown up a lot since the first book and it was great to see they faced and overcome various scenarios and obstacles that were thrown their way. I think I was in danger of seriously falling in love with Seth by the end of the story. I felt that he had really grown up in this story and it was great to see his fierce and alpha tendencies. I think that Seth is now my favourite MMA fighter book boyfriend (sorry Remy). I really liked that the book was told from both Olivia’s and Seth’s POV. It was great to finally get inside Seth’s head and learn more about his past. <br /><br />This book also has some seriously hot steamy scenes. There was a particular shower scene that was seriously hot. The story is very well written and the plot flows very well. There aren’t any OMG twists and turns but there was more than enough happening in the book to keep me hooked. Its a lovely romance story with some great MMA fighting action thrown in. <br /><br />I also enjoyed the secondary plot that featured Seth and Olivia’s best friends Jackson and Selena. Now Selena really annoyed me in book 1 but she redeemed herself in this book and although their story was told through Seth and Olivia it was great to see how their relationship was developing. I would certainly be interested in reading more about them and I think they are getting their own book soon. <br /><br />There is no cliff-hanger ending and the book ends in a great place. The epilogue at the end was particularly beautiful and moving. I really enjoyed reading this book and I’m now looking forward to the final book in the series Forever Consumed :-)<br /><br /><b>Thank you so much to author Skyla Madi for providing me with an ARC  </b> <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8739926378832718490" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_2171657657" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2171657657" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14785790455019590640">Too Consumed by Skyla Madi (Book 2 in the Consumed Series)<br/>Seth has come to the realization that Olivia is his muse, she calms him and she sees something in him that nobody else ever has. Olivia world has been turned up-side down since the passing of her father. She has had to be there for her mom. At the same time she knows that she is in love with Seth. Seth has bought Olivia fathers gym which leads to some steamy moments. Seth has made it to the pro and needs to train but when an old enemy fro</span>
  <span id="freeText14785790455019590640" style="display:none">Too Consumed by Skyla Madi (Book 2 in the Consumed Series)<br />Seth has come to the realization that Olivia is his muse, she calms him and she sees something in him that nobody else ever has. Olivia world has been turned up-side down since the passing of her father. She has had to be there for her mom. At the same time she knows that she is in love with Seth. Seth has bought Olivia fathers gym which leads to some steamy moments. Seth has made it to the pro and needs to train but when an old enemy from the past tries to sabotage him and his team, can he let it go? Olivia decides to show how she is willing to stick up for her man. Overall this was a cute read. There was not a lot of drama or rising climax, it was just a sweet read of a bad boy falling in love with a good girl and how she has changed his ways. He is still the arrogant, cocky, Seth that we all fell in love with. However in this book we get to see his softer side when it comes to Olivia, we also get to see his possessive side. The writing flowed and was easy to read. The story was a tad slow however the sizzling chemistry made up for it.<br />Hot Books &amp; Sassy Girls Blog<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12381669270611385104"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18482979.Too_Consumed__Consumed___2_' title='Too Consumed (Consumed, #2) by Skyla Madi' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1381134707s/18482979.jpg' alt='Too Consumed (Consumed, #2) by Skyla Madi' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I have been waiting MONTHS for <b>Too Consumed</b> to come out and play! And I have to say, we played and had some good ol, dirty, romantic, fun LOL<br/><br/><a href='http://s146.photobucket.com/user/latinanegra/media/post-21312-Katy-Perry-happy-dance-gif-bab-cZSf.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060145ra/7980590.gif' alt=' photo post-21312-Katy-Perry-happy-dance-gif-bab-cZSf.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>This was a great continuation of Seth and Olivia's love story. Usually second books in a series are a bit of a disappointment, but I was quite content with the happenings in this one.<br/><br/>Seth has many revelations as he starts to question many things he's done in his life (i.e. manwhoring, drinking, fighting, slutting it up) and has to come to grips that</span>
  <span id="freeText12381669270611385104" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18482979.Too_Consumed__Consumed___2_" title="Too Consumed (Consumed, #2) by Skyla Madi" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1381134707s/18482979.jpg" alt="Too Consumed (Consumed, #2) by Skyla Madi" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I have been waiting MONTHS for <b>Too Consumed</b> to come out and play! And I have to say, we played and had some good ol, dirty, romantic, fun LOL<br><br><a href="http://s146.photobucket.com/user/latinanegra/media/post-21312-Katy-Perry-happy-dance-gif-bab-cZSf.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060145ra/7980590.gif" alt=" photo post-21312-Katy-Perry-happy-dance-gif-bab-cZSf.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>This was a great continuation of Seth and Olivia's love story. Usually second books in a series are a bit of a disappointment, but I was quite content with the happenings in this one.<br><br>Seth has many revelations as he starts to question many things he's done in his life (i.e. manwhoring, drinking, fighting, slutting it up) and has to come to grips that he does in fact deserve Olivia. He struggles to make amends with all that he's done wrong and has to learn to accept that he has finally found the one person who makes him complete.<br><br>Seth is just so damn dreamy...and sexy...and hot...and oh so delicious...<br><br>We also get to see a bit more of Olivia's feistiness (which I applaud) and holding her man down is her main goal. She wants everything to do with Seth, allows him to consume her thoughts, her actions, her being, her existence.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>When you meet someone who makes your entire body buzz with one a curl of their lips, you can't escape it. You become drawn to it, forgetting everything that's supposed to matter to you. Seth became my sun and I gravitated around him - I still do, and like the sun, there's still so much to learn about Seth. I know he's big and beautiful, but I also know he's fiery and unpredictable.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s146.photobucket.com/user/latinanegra/media/tumblr_m3f5ooBQWI1r84uut.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060348ra/7980640.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_m3f5ooBQWI1r84uut.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Seth does everything in his power to convince both Olivia and himself that this is it for him. She is his one and only - and damnit, he does a mighty fine job of letting it be known.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Because I love you and I've never loved anyone before...I don't want anyone else to feel how you make me feel. I told you when we met that I'm fucking selfish and spoiled, and I wasn't kidding. I want everyone of your smiles, every laugh, every tear, every-fucking-thing - all of it - I want it and I want it all to myself."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s146.photobucket.com/user/latinanegra/media/feels-my-emotions.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1389060145ra/7980592.gif" alt=" photo feels-my-emotions.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>There is some drama that goes on. I still don't like Selena (no really, how is she and Olivia really best friends??? She is so freaking selfish it's not even funny)...and you will ooh and ahh your way through this book.<br><br>It ends in a bit of cliffhanger...but nothing too crazy. Skyla left us with some happy endings to keep us quiet until the next one comes along.<br><br>OH! And there is a ton of foreplay, lots of sexiness and holy moly-- the sex....<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>I'm stopped as he yanks my hand away. I squirm as he presses it against the cage and his free hand slips into my dress, clamping on my bare hip.<br>"Why here? Why can't you wait until we get home?"<br>He lowers his head, bringing his full lips to my ear. His breath hits my face and it's like fire lapping at my nerves, singeing and burning my insides.<br>"Why wait?" he breathes, his hand tightening around my hip. "I fight here and I want to fuck here."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><a href="http://s146.photobucket.com/user/latinanegra/media/tumblr_latgaeVWWO1qaizkuo1_500.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_886527191" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/886527191" />
    <a title="Liv" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17337105-liv"><img alt="Liv" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1386997050p2/17337105.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/886527191?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liv" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liv" href="/user/show/17337105-liv">Liv</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17337105-liv?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17337105-liv?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17337105-liv?shelf=mma-romance">mma-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer886527191" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15015764431128776742">Let's start off with the positives…..<br/><br/>I really enjoyed "Consumed" and was excited to pick up on where the first book left off in Seth and Olivia's story. It started off well enough as the reader is ushered into this world of MMA fighting as Seth is preparing for his first fight in the professional league in Vegas. Olivia and Seth are fresh in their relationship and quite in love. In the last book Seth bought Olivia's deceased father's gym and hired her to manage it. This set up was quite convenie</span>
  <span id="freeText15015764431128776742" style="display:none">Let's start off with the positives…..<br /><br />I really enjoyed "Consumed" and was excited to pick up on where the first book left off in Seth and Olivia's story. It started off well enough as the reader is ushered into this world of MMA fighting as Seth is preparing for his first fight in the professional league in Vegas. Olivia and Seth are fresh in their relationship and quite in love. In the last book Seth bought Olivia's deceased father's gym and hired her to manage it. This set up was quite convenient for the lovers as they got the opportunity to engage in their sexy banter, playful moments and to serve as a support group for one another. And, their sexual chemistry is really good. Both Seth and Olivia speak very fondly of one another and are always talking about how attracted they are to one another------ So where was the problem????<br /><br />The problem is that something was off in the energy level of both sexual and the general scenes in this book. The sexual scenes were frustrating most of the times. First of all, the abstinence between Seth and Olivia was overdrawn and just ridiculous. How frustrating that Jackson and Selina (Seth and Olivia's best friends) have a more interesting and plentiful sex life than the leads. So, when Seth and Olivia finally come together, it's rather anticlimactic….and who enjoys anticlimactic sex scenes????? There were a few sex scenes where both lovers enjoyed themselves equally, but otherwise the sex scenes seemed to be stilted and Seth held back….which was just weird. <br /><br />Another problem is that Olivia came across as a stick in the mud. What??- She'd rather go to her room and finish her book instead of celebrate with Seth post-win, leaving him to celebrate with Jackson, Selina and his crew alone….AND in Vegas????? What the??? There were other times when Olivia just came across as childish, petulant and preferred solitude when she should have worked it out quickly with her man. On the flip side, I still really liked Seth in this book. I don't mind flaws in the leads and, believe me, both Seth and Olivia have many flaws, but overall Seth's character was a lot more likable than Olivia's. This book showcased vintage Seth; he's confident, speaks his mind, can be demanding, but he's also sweet and likes to work things out by talking things through. Even Seth's jealous, overprotective side was likable. <br /><br />Also, most of the general scenes were "off," in that, Madi didn't really allow the reader to enjoy the highs in this book because each scene where there is a fabulous high seemed to be weighed down by a crappy low. I also thought the parts with Mason and Blade's interaction with Olivia was also anticlimactic. <br /><br />Overall, I was disappointed with this book, but most of all I was really frustrated……like it put me in a bad mood-frustrated. I haven't given up though, I still plan to read the final installment Forever Consumed when it is released. <br /><br />Narrator: Em Eldridge was excellent! She did a fabulous job with both Seth and Olivia's voices. <br /><br />Lastly, I hated the use of the F-word inserted in between Jesus Christ (so unnecessary and offensive). I hope this is not a trend among authors….</span>
  <a data-text-id="15015764431128776742" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/902201338?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie" href="/user/show/8201690-carrie">Carrie</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer902201338" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer16586576689692527366">Is there a better word than fabulous? If so, just insert that here. : )<br/><br/>I am not a fan of series about the same ppl, because I want the HEA and I don't like a lot of unnecessary drama, and a lot of times (most of the time) that's how those kinds of series feel to me. Skyla Madi didn't do that. She gave us a fully fleshed out HEA in Consumed, and then, in Too Consumed, it's just the continuation of that HEA. It's about Seth & Olivia after the I Love You's, about how they navigate their relationshi</span>
  <span id="freeText16586576689692527366" style="display:none">Is there a better word than fabulous? If so, just insert that here. : )<br /><br />I am not a fan of series about the same ppl, because I want the HEA and I don't like a lot of unnecessary drama, and a lot of times (most of the time) that's how those kinds of series feel to me. Skyla Madi didn't do that. She gave us a fully fleshed out HEA in Consumed, and then, in Too Consumed, it's just the continuation of that HEA. It's about Seth &amp; Olivia after the I Love You's, about how they navigate their relationship &amp; what it means to them as Seth starts his career w/ the MMAC. There's no 3rd party interference into their relationship. They still communicate openly with each other - Olivia even point out at one point that she doesn't want miscommunication to to hinder their relationship.<br /><br />There are some things going on with Seth's career and even a bit with his past that cause some moments, but they are just that - moments. They aren't used to create a break-up or anything of that sort. Their love for each other isn't questioned, and because of that we get a really compelling and emotion-driven story that doesn't mess with the HEA we were all so happy to have in the first book. <br /><br />*happy sigh* Now... when can I get my hands on book 3? : ) </span>
  <a data-text-id="16586576689692527366" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12397824130544516821">VERY GOOD FOLLOW UP BOOK<br/><br/>This is the second book in this series and I believe there is another to follow this. It was lovely to read more of Seth and Olivia, this time Seth is preparing for a big fight in LA. Olivia is supportive of Seth, she now manages her late fathers gym where Seth trains.<br/>Characters from the first book also feature, including Selena Olivia's BF and Jackson Seth's friend.   <span id="freeText12397824130544516821" style="display:none">VERY GOOD FOLLOW UP BOOK<br /><br />This is the second book in this series and I believe there is another to follow this. It was lovely to read more of Seth and Olivia, this time Seth is preparing for a big fight in LA. Olivia is supportive of Seth, she now manages her late fathers gym where Seth trains.<br />Characters from the first book also feature, including Selena Olivia's BF and Jackson Seth's friend. The sub plot involving them was an added bonus. Jackson has some serious baggage from his past, so I expect there will be more of that in the next book.<br /><br />Seth is as sexy and possessive as ever but this time round we get to see his more vulnerable side to his character which was nice. Olivia is as loyal and protective of Seth as he is of her. I really liked the way they communicated and sorted out any problems between them as and when that happened that was a refreshing change not to have long and drawn out misunderstandings. As usual the love scenes are really hot and passionate. Seth's main enemy rears his ugly head again providing the drama. I'm really looking forward to the next book.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer11259498889272631801">Loved it! Here's me thinking that the first book was a stand alone but was surprised to see a second book in the series.   <span id="freeText11259498889272631801" style="display:none">Loved it! Here's me thinking that the first book was a stand alone but was surprised to see a second book in the series. I loved Seth &amp; Olivia in Consumed but after reading this book I love them even more. Your given more insight into their relationship and reading about them develop was an absolute pleasure. Let's hope the final book Don gets what's coming to him. I cannot express how highly I love these books. Recommend! You won't be disappointed. 5 STARS *****</span>
  <a data-text-id="11259498889272631801" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('FmkMvGG0HPLusgIfQWUys6fBImEmEmuctmcVomj5s6vuJPfD8QGNuLQ/1uNKUNZHq6EwdS5j8XU8waT0w4o3Ag==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('kGeOKHdZY1AClxcSKXNjn6f6Exovy5Rp2ZhXHuxPGJloKnVX5+zyGlgaw+4iRodrq5oBDie6DoBTPuZIRzycMA==')})
  }
